< Review>
Had a frustrating experience. Rented a used textbook from the bookstore. It came in poor condition and it had water damage and some pages we're suspiciously stuck together. I thought nothing of it because it was a used rental. Turns out the book was useless for the class and was hardly used it at all during the semester and it spent the majority of the time in my desk drawer. Overall a waste of money renting it. When attempting to return the book, I was told that they would not accept the book in the condition, the same exact condition I received the book. I was told i would have to buy the book or be subjected to late fees. Ended up buying it for only $6. While it was clearly not a large amount of money, the fact that the bookstore sends out used books in poor condition and the refuses to accept them in the same exact condition is both frustrating and unethical. If the bookstore really cares about the condition of the books they sell, they would do a better job at checking the condition of the books before they send them out to students and give them the run around when they are simply trying to return the books on time. I will never rent textbooks from the bookstore again.<//Review>

<user_id>105234362170523652866<//user_id><username>andrew saetern< /username><time>1533622085759</time><Rate>3< /Rate>< Review>
Beautiful rooftop restaurant. Lovely D√©cor and view. It's a great place to go to enjoy the weather, people watch, and grab something eat (if it arrives). My friend lives just a few blocks away, and we were starving after a visit to the USS Midway. Although he comes here often for dinners and events, he had never been for lunch. Long story short....our lunch took about 50 minutes to arrive. We ordered the Poke and Avocado Toast as appetizers. Sadly all of our dishes arrived at the same time.... yes, even the Avocado Toast. We also had the Tacos and Buffalo Chicken Wrap. The food is decent, but I'm not impressed with the service here. We quickly ate our lunch and left. What we thought would be a short lunch ended up taking much longer, and we had a dog to walk.  Our server had to fill our iced teas more times than I can remember.

To make up for the long wait for our food, the server didn't charge us for appetizers. That was nice of them. I think they could have done better with the food situation. There were a whole lot of staff walking around. Most of them looked like management. It even looked like they were have a little meeting near the bar.

Did I mention that all of their servers are attractive? I wonder what their interview process is like. Do they show up in swimsuits? :-) lol.<//Review>

<username>Marlon Maus DrPH MD</username><Time>1615858369578<//Time><rating>4<//rating>< Review>
What can one say? Safeway is Safeway! This one is not especially better or worse than any other Safeway. It has all the usual items we expect Safeway to have. You will find lots of cans and cereals and paper towels and tomato sauces. It has the usual baked goods, cheese selection, and butcher. What does distinguish this Safeway for many others I have visited is the small plaza they built at a time when lots of people could gather in a socially not very distant way. Today there are no chairs just a few tables that are cemented to the floor. However, being able to sit in the plaza and watch people go bye really makes sheltering in place a lot easier. So thanks Safeway for thinking of the community when you designed this store!</Review>

< review>
It's a Safeway, so it's a mixed bag. They have enough of the important things, and the hours are certainly convenient.

It's not the worse Safeway ever, but it's not the best.

Still, it's really a pedestrian area.

It's a bit of an eyesore, and it blocks the view of the hills.

And having a big supermarket here makes the traffic even worse than it was.

The parking lot is often full, which means the streets nearby get clogged with people trying to parallel park.

It would have been so nice to have had a park here.<//review>

< Text>
Great that its 24hrs... but other than that, the workers don't have the best customer service (they often seem in a bad mood, even when I thank them at check out), and the store layout is compact, making it hard to navigate shopping carts when busy. This Safeway (6310 College Ave, Berkeley, CA) is open 24/7 and took 1.5 years to rebuild and expand with rooftop parking and elevator to store on ground level.  Grand re-opening was in 2015.  The bakery is a favorite of mine.  If you're an insomniac like me and love fresh baked bread, pick up warm rolls, baguettes or French bread as early as 4 AM and breakfast pastries and doughnuts around 6 AM.  They restock shelves and produce throughout the nite and they're always friendly about rainchecks if out of stock.<//review>
